 Indeed, the face of the world is changing and like the magazine that has kept a finger on the beats of the country and the world for the last 40 years, this conclave will also take stock of the activities on the domestic and external front
 vichaaron or daleelon ke is utsav main har kshetra kii behtareen or vilakshan shakhsiyaten apni baat rakhengi

 india today patrika immergency ke dauraan shuru hui thi

 is baar apni bolne kii aazaadee ke liye aalochana kaa shikaar hui eibi toli ko bhi vivaad bhadakne ke baad pehali baar apni baat rakhane kaa mauka milegaa
 The conclave is also a platform for the reception of new ideas
